    general

    Display a listing of Banner model

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/banners/lists" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/banners/lists",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    Example response:

    {
    "banners": [
        {
            "id": 1,
            "title": "ProleÄ‡ni",
            "link": "https:\/\/www.google.rs\/",
            "image": "storage\/uploads\/banners\/08-2018\/prolecni-1-sQ.jpg",
            "width": 600,
            "height": 180,
            "is_visible": 1,
            "created_at": "2018-07-13 19:38:36",
            "updated_at": "2018-08-11 21:37:21"
        }
    ]
}

    HTTP Request

    GET api/banners

    HEAD api/banners

    method used to store a newly created Banner model

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/banners" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="minima" \
    -d "link"="minima" \
    -d "image"="minima" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/banners",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "title": "minima",
        "link": "minima",
        "image": "minima"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/partners/{partner}

    HEAD api/partners/{partner}

    Update the specified resource in storage.

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/partners/{partner}" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="et" \
    -d "slug"="et" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/partners/{partner}",
    "method": "PUT",
    "data": {
        "title": "et",
        "slug": "et"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/partners/{partner}

    PATCH api/partners/{partner}

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    title string required
    slug string required

    method used to remove the specified Partner model

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/partners/{partner}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/partners/{partner}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/permissions

    HEAD api/permissions

    method used to store new Permission model

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/permissions" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "permission_group_id"="43" \
    -d "name"="neque" \
    -d "guard_name"="neque" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/permissions",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "permission_group_id": 43,
        "name": "neque",
        "guard_name": "neque"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/permission-groups/lists

    HEAD api/permission-groups/lists

    method used to return lists of PermissionGroup model

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/permission-groups" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/permission-groups",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/posts/lists

    HEAD api/posts/lists

    Display a listing of Post model

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/posts" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/posts",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/posts

    HEAD api/posts

    method used to store new post and return

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/posts" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="modi" \
    -d "slug"="modi" \
    -d "short"="modi" \
    -d "image"="modi" \
    -d "image_box"="modi" \
    -d "blog_ids"="modi" \
    -d "publish_at"="1980-11-02" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/posts",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "title": "modi",
        "slug": "modi",
        "short": "modi",
        "image": "modi",
        "image_box": "modi",
        "blog_ids": "modi",
        "publish_at": "1980-11-02"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/products

    HEAD api/products

    method used to store new product and return

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/products" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="sed" \
    -d "slug"="sed" \
    -d "link"="sed" \
    -d "brand_id"="sed" \
    -d "gender_id"="sed" \
    -d "category_ids"="sed" \
    -d "image"="sed" \
    -d "price"="254640171" \
    -d "outlet_price"="254640171" \
    -d "code"="sed" \
    -d "publish_at"="1975-10-07" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/products",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "title": "sed",
        "slug": "sed",
        "link": "sed",
        "brand_id": "sed",
        "gender_id": "sed",
        "category_ids": "sed",
        "image": "sed",
        "price": 254640171,
        "outlet_price": 254640171,
        "code": "sed",
        "publish_at": "1975-10-07"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST api/products

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    title string required
    slug string required
    link string required
    brand_id string required
    gender_id string required
    category_ids string required
    image image optional Must be an image (jpeg, png, bmp, gif, or svg) Allowed mime types: jpg, jpeg, png or gif
    price numeric required Minimum: 1
    outlet_price numeric optional Minimum: 0
    code string required
    publish_at date required

    method used to return product

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/products/{product}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/products/{product}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/products/{product}

    HEAD api/products/{product}

    method used to update product and return

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/products/{product}" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="est" \
    -d "slug"="est" \
    -d "link"="est" \
    -d "brand_id"="est" \
    -d "gender_id"="est" \
    -d "category_ids"="est" \
    -d "image"="est" \
    -d "price"="1303178685" \
    -d "outlet_price"="1303178685" \
    -d "code"="est" \
    -d "publish_at"="1999-07-02" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/products/{product}",
    "method": "PUT",
    "data": {
        "title": "est",
        "slug": "est",
        "link": "est",
        "brand_id": "est",
        "gender_id": "est",
        "category_ids": "est",
        "image": "est",
        "price": 1303178685,
        "outlet_price": 1303178685,
        "code": "est",
        "publish_at": "1999-07-02"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/products/{product}

    PATCH api/products/{product}

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    title string required
    slug string required
    link string required
    brand_id string required
    gender_id string required
    category_ids string required
    image image optional Must be an image (jpeg, png, bmp, gif, or svg) Allowed mime types: jpg, jpeg, png or gif
    price numeric required Minimum: 1
    outlet_price numeric optional Minimum: 0
    code string required
    publish_at date required

    method used to destroy product

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/products/{product}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/products/{product}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/roles

    HEAD api/roles

    method used to store new Role model

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/roles" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "name"="sint" \
    -d "guard_name"="sint" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/roles",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "name": "sint",
        "guard_name": "sint"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST api/roles

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required
    guard_name string required

    method used to return Role model

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/roles/{role}

    HEAD api/roles/{role}

    method used to update Role model

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "name"="consectetur" \
    -d "guard_name"="consectetur" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}",
    "method": "PUT",
    "data": {
        "name": "consectetur",
        "guard_name": "consectetur"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/roles/{role}

    PATCH api/roles/{role}

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    name string required
    guard_name string required

    method used to destroy Role model

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/roles/{role}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/roles/{role}

    method used to save permissions to current Role model

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/roles/{id}/permissions" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/roles/{id}/permissions",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST api/roles/{id}/permissions

    method used to return Setting model

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/settings/{id}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/settings/{id}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/statistics/{id}/day

    HEAD api/statistics/{id}/day

    method used to return clicks in month day

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/statistics/{id}/month" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/statistics/{id}/month",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/statistics/{id}/month

    HEAD api/statistics/{id}/month

    method used to return clicks in last year

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/statistics/{id}/year" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/statistics/{id}/year",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    HEAD api/statistics/{id}/year

    var settings = {

    HTTP Request

    GET api/subscribers

    HEAD api/subscribers

    Store a newly created resource in storage.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/subscribers" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "email"="tanya.koepp@example.org" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/subscribers",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "email": "tanya.koepp@example.org"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST api/subscribers

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    email email required

    Display the specified resource.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/subscribers/{subscriber}

    HEAD api/subscribers/{subscriber}

    Update the specified resource in storage.

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "email"="christop95@example.net" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}",
    "method": "PUT",
    "data": {
        "email": "christop95@example.net"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/subscribers/{subscriber}

    PATCH api/subscribers/{subscriber}

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    email email required

    Remove the specified resource from storage.

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"

    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/subscribers/{subscriber}",

    "headers": {

    console.log(response);

    HTTP Request

    GET api/tags

    HEAD api/tags

    method used to store new tag and return

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/tags" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="sed" \
    -d "slug"="sed" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tags",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "title": "sed",
        "slug": "sed"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET api/tags/{tag}

    HEAD api/tags/{tag}

    method used to update tag and return

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT "http://localhost/api/tags/{tag}" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "title"="ducimus" \
    -d "slug"="ducimus" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tags/{tag}",
    "method": "PUT",
    "data": {
        "title": "ducimus",
        "slug": "ducimus"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    PUT api/tags/{tag}

    PATCH api/tags/{tag}

    Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    title string required
    slug string required

    method used to destroy tag

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE "http://localhost/api/tags/{tag}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/tags/{tag}",
    "method": "DELETE",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    DELETE api/tags/{tag}

    method used to search tags paginate by 50

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/tags/search" \
-H "Accept: application/json"

    HTTP Request

    GET api/users

    HEAD api/users

    method used to store new user and return

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/api/users" \
-H "Accept: application/json" \
    -d "name"="ut" \
    -d "email"="nakia.mcclure@example.org" \
    -d "password"="ut" \

    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/api/users",
    "method": "POST",
    "data": {
        "name": "ut",
        "email": "nakia.mcclure@example.org",
        "password": "ut"
},
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
